msg:I was watching a concert at the Olympic Sports Center, so I booked the nearest Sheraton. The location of the hotel is really great. You can see the Olympic Sports Center from the floor-to-ceiling windows of the room, and you can enter the venue in less than 10 minutes' walk. It's raining heavily. If you stay here, you don't have to worry about traffic jams or difficulty calling a taxi after the show. It takes about 30 minutes to reach scenic spots like Daming Lake and Jinan East Railway Station by online taxi. The hotel service is very good, the front desk is decent and attentive, and the doorman is also very enthusiastic to help with luggage. The breakfast is also quite rich, with many choices of Chinese, Western and Japanese styles. It was not a holiday when I checked in, so there were a lot of people, but the corridor was very quiet and the overall experience was very good.
